        var windowWidth = window.innerWidth
          , smallScreen = 767
          , searchForm = document.getElementsByClassName("search-box-container-collapsed")[0]
          , desktopParent = document.getElementById("desktop-search-bar-container")
          , mobileParent = document.getElementById("mobile-search-bar-container");

        if ( windowWidth <= smallScreen ) {

            if ( searchForm.parentNode.id != "mobile-search-bar-container" ) {
                mobileParent.append(searchForm);
            }
        } else {

            if ( searchForm.parentNode.id != "desktop-search-bar-container" ) {
                desktopParent.append(searchForm);
            }
        }
    };

    changeSearchContainer();
    window.onresize = changeSearchContainer;
    

</script>


        <!-- Anchors used by `aria-describedby` states -->
        <div id="wayfinding" class="squelch">
            <span id="current-site">Current site</span>
            <span id="current-page">Current page</span>
        </div>

        <script type="text/javascript">

            // Find touch devices
            document.addEventListener('touchstart', function addtouchclass(e){ // first time user touches the screen
                document.documentElement.classList.add('can-touch') // add "can-touch" class to document root using classList API
                document.removeEventListener('touchstart', addtouchclass, false) // de-register touchstart event
            }, false)

            $('.nav-toggle').on('click', function() { $('.app-nav').addClass('open'); });
            $('.close-nav').on('click', function() { $('.app-nav').removeClass('open'); });
        </script>
        
    </body>
</html>
